MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Grandstander-Thin', Everything looks good.

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. Grandstander Thin Regular (Grandstander[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Grandstander' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Thin' = NID 1 'Grandstander Thin'.

Pass

Grandstander Thin Regular (Grandstander[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16

Reserved word used in Typographic Family Name NID16 and not allowed in Microsoft Office applications.

NID 16 does not contain any of the following keywords: 'Book, Ultra, Normal'

Pass

Grandstander Thin Regular (Grandstander[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 17

Name table entry according Monotype

NID 16 and 17 is not required for a variable font. In case you have good reasons, please keep it, otherwise please remove it.

Grandstander Thin Regular (Grandstander[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 25

Reserved word used in Variations PostScript Name Prefix NID25

Entry: 'GrandstanderRoman'
The keyword 'Roman' may cause issues in Microsoft Office applications. Style linking and/or font embedding for MS Word won't work.
(The keyword 'Roman' causes cross platform issues in Adobe InDesign, Jan. 2019)
More infos here:
Unified Monotype Weight Name Rules

Pass

Grandstander Thin Italic (Grandstander-Italic[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Grandstander-ThinItalic', Everything looks good.

Grandstander Thin Italic (Grandstander-Italic[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Grandstander' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Thin Italic' = NID 1 'Grandstander Thin' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Underline Position and Thickness

Underline Position and Thickness

Pass

Grandstander Thin Regular (Grandstander[wght].ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-100'.
underlineThicknes is '50'.

Pass

Grandstander Thin Italic (Grandstander-Italic[wght].ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-100'.
underlineThicknes is '50'.

gasp

Default

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
